<div id="review_1115805034" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1115805034" />
    <a title="Mairéad (is roaming the Undying Lands)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9184362-mair-ad-is-roaming-the-undying-lands"><img alt="Mairéad (is roaming the Undying Lands)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1472748159p2/9184362.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1115805034?book_show_action=true">Nov 26, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mairéad (is roaming the Undying Lands)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mairéad (is roaming the Undying Lands)" href="/user/show/9184362-mair-ad-is-roaming-the-undying-lands">Mairéad (is roaming the Undying Lands)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1115805034" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9715179215993347213"><b>{December 8th, 2014} MINI-REVIEW</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“In short, heroism means doing the right thing regardless of the consequences.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>2.5 stars (ouch much?).<br/><br/>Apparently I never did the review or update for this one, my bad. Been so scatterbrained lately with all the preparations for Christmas and my trip that will beginning on December 21st. It has been absolutely <i>insane</i> as of late! And I think another reason why I hadn't done anything about this book was because it felt so meh. And here it started out so promising</span>
  <span id="freeText9715179215993347213" style="display:none"><b>{December 8th, 2014} MINI-REVIEW</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>“In short, heroism means doing the right thing regardless of the consequences.”</i>
</b><br /><br />2.5 stars (ouch much?).<br /><br />Apparently I never did the review or update for this one, my bad. Been so scatterbrained lately with all the preparations for Christmas and my trip that will beginning on December 21st. It has been absolutely <i>insane</i> as of late! And I think another reason why I hadn't done anything about this book was because it felt so meh. And here it started out so promising...<br /><br />The characters, especially main character #1 Jason Walker, felt smarter and improved from Mull's other series I had been reading <i>Fablehaven</i>, unfortunately I found out in the next few chapters that I favoured the main characters of <i>Fablehaven</i> much more. It's an ironic twist of fate in my opinion, especially with how I had such a problem with them (if you've read my review of the first Fablehaven book, and my updates of the next two books, you'd see why).<br /><br />But perhaps my main problem with this book was that it felt so flat, and lifeless compared to its precursor. Looki, I know he had been working on this book for so long, years and years of drafting--but maybe that's where it felt short? I mean, the writing has really improved and you can tell how much work was put into it. However that might be what resulted in this sort of flat and lifeless overall story and its characters. Like I was reading along but it just felt so <i>meh</i> that it just broke my heart. Probably why I was neglecting this book over the 3rd book of the Fablehaven series.<br /><br />However, since I have have the entire series to read, it would be a shame to merely stop here. Especially when it is interesting to see how this turns out. I still hold out that I'll find some life in these pages that will draw me into the story rather than merely acting as an observer. x:<br /><br /><i>
  <b>“For each of us destiny is a blend of potential, circumstances, and choices.”</b>
</i><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9715179215993347213" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/104809001" />
    <a title="Erica (storybookend)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2835464-erica-storybookend"><img alt="Erica (storybookend)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595779045p2/2835464.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/104809001?book_show_action=true">May 29, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Erica (storybookend)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Erica (storybookend)" href="/user/show/2835464-erica-storybookend">Erica (storybookend)</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2835464-erica-storybookend?shelf=love-love-it">love-love-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2835464-erica-storybookend?shelf=i-own">i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2835464-erica-storybookend?shelf=2011-reads">2011-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2835464-erica-storybookend?shelf=lds-authors">lds-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2835464-erica-storybookend?shelf=release-in-2011">release-in-2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2835464-erica-storybookend?shelf=made-me-laugh">made-me-laugh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2835464-erica-storybookend?shelf=original-creative-premise">original-creative-premise</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer104809001" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4076497865584965645">Well, quite a fantastic adventure I must say! <i>A World Without Heroes</i> is certainly a very imaginative, creative story in a very intriguing, strange world. It will definitely appeal to all Fablehaven fans (and if it doesn’t, well something must be wrong with you ;), and pretty much any young teenager looking for a fantastical adventure. I really enjoyed reading it. <br/><br/>The two main characters, Jason and Rachel, are two teenagers who unintentionally get sucked from our world into a whole new, magical w</span>
  <span id="freeText4076497865584965645" style="display:none">Well, quite a fantastic adventure I must say! <i>A World Without Heroes</i> is certainly a very imaginative, creative story in a very intriguing, strange world. It will definitely appeal to all Fablehaven fans (and if it doesn’t, well something must be wrong with you ;), and pretty much any young teenager looking for a fantastical adventure. I really enjoyed reading it. <br /><br />The two main characters, Jason and Rachel, are two teenagers who unintentionally get sucked from our world into a whole new, magical world run by an evil wizard (the only one there is in fact), and find themselves searching for the Word that will destroy this dark wizard. This Word supposedly will be the undoing of Maldor when spoken in his presence. But very few people know of it‘s existence and none knowing the whole word. It is broken up into syllables hidden across the Lyrian land. Jason and Rachel must search for these syllables, going through unimaginable circumstances and surviving against all odds to succeed.<br /><br />Brandon Mull created a fantastic world, with interesting people and creatures, crafting an epic adventure that was extremely well planned and executed (it is after all a story 10 years in the making). Granted, this novel is geared towards younger teenagers, not older teenagers and adults who prefer thought provoking books with deep emotion and romance. This book is purely for fun, and I loved it! . (a little gripe, Jason seemed too astute and wise for a 13 year old. He spoke like he was from Lyrian and had grown up with extensive learning and learning extremely well manners, not just a normal teenager from our world. In any case, he had his sense of humor that made me laugh sometimes). I loved this first installment in the Beyonders series, it certainly lived up to my expectations, but I will stand by my loyalty to <i>Fablehaven</i> which I deem much more incredible and epic! </span>
  <a data-text-id="4076497865584965645" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/161412315" />
    <a title="Tish" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4968277-tish"><img alt="Tish" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1319660468p2/4968277.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/161412315?book_show_action=true">Apr 16, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tish" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tish" href="/user/show/4968277-tish">Tish</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer161412315" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15961880427617935182">I didn't enjoy this nearly as much as I enjoyed Brandon Mull's Fablehaven series. There didn't seem to be much character development so that even by the end of the story, I didn't really care what happened to the main characters. In addition, the author didn't really seem to build up any suspense so that the big "shocker" at the end wasn't. Jason, the main character, says he is totally wiped out by what he learns, but I never felt it. Also, I would have preferred to find out more about the links</span>
  <span id="freeText15961880427617935182" style="display:none">I didn't enjoy this nearly as much as I enjoyed Brandon Mull's Fablehaven series. There didn't seem to be much character development so that even by the end of the story, I didn't really care what happened to the main characters. In addition, the author didn't really seem to build up any suspense so that the big "shocker" at the end wasn't. Jason, the main character, says he is totally wiped out by what he learns, but I never felt it. Also, I would have preferred to find out more about the links between this new world and our world, the whys and wherefores, even just some hints, to make me feel like there was a bigger story (to be revealed at some point in future books in the series, perhaps) behind what was happening in this one.<br /><br />Now, my son, age 11, says he quite enjoyed it and would give it 3.75 stars to Fablehaven's 4 stars and that he is eager to read the second in the series once it is released.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15961880427617935182" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ZpC1tyy7Rs5V7sByvJuBqPG50JPdsmZgAlYRsYbqKQOjVb11CMHMPxTLuw7Yiwcq2Z2foOynffmictghz2ziJw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('AEoB1aRBok2OKGEol+LQDQ+vbJVmiI8VVSALonjoVKvFjwkXgDsovM8NGlTz8laPJ4sjpledlIz1BMIyMW6fjw==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
